<!-- --> <div class="feed-shared-update-v2__description-wrapper ember-view" id="ember372" style=""><div class="feed-shared-inline-show-more-text feed-shared-update-v2__description feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--minimal-padding ember-view" id="ember373" tabindex="-1"> <div class="feed-shared-text relative feed-shared-update-v2__commentary ember-view" dir="ltr" id="ember374"><!-- -->
<span class="break-words">
<span><span dir="ltr">As we gear up for covid 2.0 anxiety, here's a look at how covid is messing up with our brains:<br/><br/>Neuroscientists have traced our habit-making behaviors to a part of the brain called the basal ganglia, which also plays a key role in the development of emotions, memories and pattern recognition.<br/><br/>Decisions, meanwhile, are made in a different part of the brain called the prefrontal cortex (PFC).<br/><br/>But as soon as a behavior becomes automatic, the decision-making part of your brain goes into a sleep mode of sorts. So, once you have practiced driving again and again, it becomes a reflex for you and doesnt take much mental bandwidth. Same for your daily chores - you don't have to think them, you do them on autopilot.<br/><br/>Utilizing PFC takes a lot of energy and if we have to use it frequently, we get tired. In covid, our routine life is disrupted and hence, basal ganglia cant control it. We have to activate our PFC again and again and it exhausts us!<br/><br/>Now that we get this, what can we do to not let the stress get to us-<br/>1. Write a list of things you are grateful for - helps combat FOMO &amp; anxiety<br/>2. Schedule your mental energy intensive tasks when you are fresh/alert eg. morning<br/>3. Slow down &amp; meditate<br/><br/><a data-attribute-index="0" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=mentalhealth&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788713562471718912">#mentalhealth</a> <a data-attribute-index="1" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=covid&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788713562471718912">#covid</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<!-- --> <div class="feed-shared-update-v2__description-wrapper ember-view" id="ember700" style=""><div class="feed-shared-inline-show-more-text feed-shared-update-v2__description feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--minimal-padding ember-view" id="ember701" tabindex="-1"> <div class="feed-shared-text relative feed-shared-update-v2__commentary ember-view" dir="ltr" id="ember702"><!-- -->
<span class="break-words">
<span><span dir="ltr">Curious about whether you should apply Reinforcement Learning to the problem you are currently working on? If so, what RL algorithm: on-policy, off-policy, offline, goal-conditioned, model-based or something else? There is a substantial disconnect between the theory and practice of RL. Along with <a data-attribute-index="0" data-entity-hovercard-id="urn:li:fs_miniProfile:ACoAAACd86wBu2jqGayCrG6WS0l44nttRDblZdw" data-entity-type="MINI_PROFILE" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/ACoAAACd86wBu2jqGayCrG6WS0l44nttRDblZdw">Cathy Wu</a>, we have designed a summer course for working professionals seeking to learn how to apply RL. Check out details here:</span></span>
</span>

<span class="break-words">
<span><span dir="ltr">Self Doubt. Anxiety. Stress. Helplessness. Uncertainty. Fear. Depression. Negativity. <br/><br/>These are the uncomfortable topics we rarely discuss in the <a data-attribute-index="0" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=data&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788776691834740737">#data</a> community - and I think we should change that!<br/><br/>Times are hard but together as a community - we can all do our part to support one another and really make a difference.<br/><br/>Its as simple as reaching out to others and being yourself, authentic and genuine you.<br/><br/>Open up and embrace your vulnerability for we are all human at the end of the day <br/><br/>Ask for help, offer help and receive the blessings of positive energy.<br/><br/>Hows that for a mantra!<br/><br/>Now go get it - take action, be brave and keep on keeping on <br/><br/> <a data-attribute-index="1" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=mentalhealth&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788776691834740737">#mentalhealth</a> <a data-attribute-index="2" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=datawithdanny&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788776691834740737">#DataWithDanny</a></span></span>

<!-- --> <div class="feed-shared-update-v2__description-wrapper ember-view" id="ember1039" style=""><div class="feed-shared-inline-show-more-text feed-shared-update-v2__description feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--minimal-padding feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--5-lines ember-view" id="ember1040" tabindex="-1"> <div class="feed-shared-text relative feed-shared-update-v2__commentary ember-view" dir="ltr" id="ember1041"><!-- -->
<span class="break-words">
<span><span dir="ltr">Couple of days back I left TCS after serving for over 9 years. People keep asking me how does it feel having worked for almost a decade for one organization. Well, I can only put it this way that the feeling is very personal. It has been a wonderful journey which gave me friends and memories of a lifetime. Thank you <a data-attribute-index="0" data-entity-hovercard-id="urn:li:fs_miniCompany:1353" data-entity-type="MINI_COMPANY" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/tata-consultancy-services/">Tata Consultancy Services</a> for the potential you saw in me. Bearing the <a data-attribute-index="2" href="https://www.linkedin.com/feed/hashtag/?keywords=tcoc&amp;highlightedUpdateUrns=urn%3Ali%3Aactivity%3A6788456490677108736">#TCOC</a> in mind and in actions I will soon be taking on a new journey but the attachment with you as my first employer will remain unparalleled </span></span>
</span>
</div>
